 Today Azad is the birthday of Kodandera Madappa Kariappa (KM Kariappa), who commanded the Indian Army
 kariappa desh ke pehle commander-in-chif the
 He took over from General Roy Francis Butcher, the last British top commander of the Indian Army during the British Raj on 15 January 1949, the same day the whole country celebrates as Army Day
 unhone saal 1947 main hue bharat-paak yuddh main pashchimi seemaa par bhartiya sena kaa netritv bhi kiya
 He was born in Karnataka in 1899 and his father Kodandera was a revenue officer in Madikeri
 ghar main unhen sabhi log pyaar se ‘chimmaa’ kahkar pukaarte the
 Cariappa did his early education at Central High School in Madikeri
 shuru se hi vah padhai main bahut achche the
 He loved maths and painting very much
 saal 1917 main schuli shiksha puri karne ke baad unhone madras ke presidency kalege main admician le liya

 ve bhartiya sena ke un do adhikariyon main shaamil hai jinhen field marshall kii padavi di gai
 Field Marshal Sam Manekshaw was the second officer to be given the rank of Field Marshal
 kariappa ko 'keeper' ke naam se pukaara jaataa tha
 He is the only Indian to reach the rank of Field Marshal

 truman ne unhen 'order of the Chief Commander of the Legion of Merit' se sammanit kiya

6 million patients suffer from Alzheimer's

 dementia main kai bimaariyaan shaamil hai, jaise alzimer rog, front tu temporal dementia, vascular dementia aadi
 In dementia patients, initially memory begins to weaken and the patient starts having trouble in daily work
 marij tarikhon, raaston or jaruri kaamon ko bhuulane lagata he
 He starts making wrong decisions while working at home or office
